[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1146002
     - Topic: Stress at work
     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator that helps HR users investigate phenomena within the company.
Firstly, the user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic.
Then, the user will ask to convert it into a specified format.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. 

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Stress at work

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure thing! Here is a potential stress at work questionnaire:
```vbnet
1) How often do you feel stressed while working? (Always, Often, Sometimes, Rarely, Never)
2) On a scale of 0-10, how would rate your overall level of job satisfaction right now? Please provide the reason for this score.
3) Do you have enough time to complete tasks and projects at work or do they feel rushed/unrealistic due dates set by management team members (Yes / No)? If not then please specify what is missing in order make it more manageable timeline-wise so that we can address the issue properly? 
4) Do you have enough resources to complete tasks and projects at work or do they feel like there are constant firefighting mode due lack of materials/tools (Yes / No)? If not then please specify what is missing in order make it more manageable resource-wise so that we can address the issue properly? 
5) Do you have clear expectations about your role and responsibilities at work or do they change frequently without any notice which makes them hard to meet effectively, causing stress (Yes / No)? If not then please specify what is missing in order make it more manageable expectation-wise so that we can address the issue properly? 
6) How often are you able to take a break when needed during your workday and how long do these breaks usually last before returning back on duty again (Yes / No)? If not then please specify what is missing in order make it more manageable time-wise so that we can address the issue properly? 
7) Do people around you at workplace cause stress or help reduce this feeling by being supportive and understanding of your needs, especially during high pressure situations where deadlines are tight (Yes / No)? If not then please specify what is missing in order make it more manageable support-wise so that we can address the issue properly? 
8) How often do you feel like there's too much work coming at once and how does this affect your performance, causing stress or burnout if unchecked over time (Yes / No)? If yes then please specify what is missing in order make it more manageable volume-wise so that we can address the issue properly? 
9) Do you feel like there's a good balance between work and personal life at your current job, allowing for proper recovery from stressful situations or do they constantly overlap causing tension (Yes / No)? If not then please specify what is missing in order make it more manageable time-wise so that we can address the issue properly? 
10) How well does communication flow within teams and departments at your workplace, allowing for effective collaboration without miscommunication or misunderstanding leading to stressful situations (Yes / No)? If not then please specify what is missing in order make it more manageable time-wise so that we can address the issue properly?
```
     - User:

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1146004
     - Topic: Workplace Environment
     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator that helps HR users investigate phenomena within the company.
Firstly, the user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic.
Then, the user will ask to convert it into a specified format.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. 

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Environment

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a potential questionnaire about workplace environment:

1. How would you describe the physical space in which you work? Is it comfortable, well-lit, and conducive to productivity? Please explain your answer further if possible. (Multiple choice or open format)
2. Do you feel that there are sufficient quiet spaces for focused thinking time within this workplace environment? If not, what could be done differently so people have access to more private areas when needed? This question is asking about the availability of meeting rooms and other types of workspaces in an office setting (Multiple choice or open format)
3. How would you rate your overall satisfaction with our current food service options if available at workplace, both for quality AND variety on a scale from 1-5 where one being not satisfied to five means very much satisified? Please provide specific examples of what could be improved in the comments box below (Multiple choice or open format)
4. How often do you feel like your personal workspace is invaded by others, and how does this affect productivity negatively if at all ? This question aims for people to reflect on their need for privacy when working as well( Multiple Choice Or Open Format ) 5 . Do the current temperature settings in our workplace make it easier or harder for you do perform your job? Please explain why. (Multiple choice and open format)
6 How would rate noise level at work place ? Is there too much background chatter that makes concentration difficult,or is this not a problem because people are able to focus regardless of the environment around them?( Multiple Choice Or Open Format ) 7 . Do you feel like your workplace allows for enough flexibility and autonomy in terms setting up personal space? If no what could be done differently so employees have more control over their workspaces (Multiple choice or open format)
8. How would rate the overall cleanliness of this workspace, including things such as bathrooms on a scale from 1-5 where one being not satisfied to five means very much satisified? Please provide specific examples in comments box below if possible( Multiple Choice Or Open Format )9 . Do you feel that there are enough opportunities for collaboration and social interaction within this workplace environment, or do people tend towards isolation due lack of good design (Multiple choice OR open format)
10. How would rate the overall aesthetic appeal AND vibe OF THIS WORKPLACE ENVIRONMENT on a scale from 1-5 where one being not satisfied to five means very much satisified? Please provide specific examples in comments box below if possible( Multiple Choice Or Open Format )
Thank you for taking time out of your day and sharing with us! We appreciate all feedback.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Environment

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a potential remote work experience questionnaire:
```vbnet
1) How would you describe your overall remote work experiences? (Open-ended, multiple choice or rating scale options are all acceptable.)
2) Which tools and technologies do you use to stay connected with colleagues while working remotely? Please rank them in order of importance. Include things like email clients, chat apps, project management software etc., but also think about the physical items such as a headset for taking calls or even just your computer/laptop!
3) How often do you feel lonely when not physically present with team members? (Multiple choice: Never; Rarely-1 time per month at most; Occasionally - 2 to 5 times monthly, regularly – more than once a week.) If possible please provide an explanation for your answer. For example if it's "Never" because you have good communication channels or maybe just don’t feel lonely easily!
4) What is the biggest challenge that prevents effective remote work? (Open-ended response encouraged!) Is there anything specific about this issue which makes working remotely difficult, and how could these problems be mitigated in future if at all possible. 5) On a scale of one to ten where do you feel most comfortable with your current workspace setup for productivity purposes while remote working? (Please include any details regarding why they chose that number.)
6) How many hours per week does it take before feeling burnt out due solely from being in front-of screen time and not having enough breaks during the day. This question is particularly important because burnout can lead to decreased performance at work so understanding how much 'screen' or virtual face-to-face contact employees need might help inform better practices around remote working habits moving forward!
7) In terms of communication style, do you prefer synchronous methods like real time chat and video calls over asynchronously written emails? (Multiple choice: Yes; No. If no then please specify why not.) 8 ) Is there a specific type or size team that works best for remote work in your experience so far if any at all ? Please elaborate on reasons behind this preference, whether it's related to technology limitations/preferences OR personal preferences based upon communication styles and habits etc.
```
Please let me know which format you would like the questionnaire converted into!

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a sample questionnaire about employee ONBOARDING process:

1. How would you describe the current onboarding program for new hires? Is it structured or unstructured, and does this vary based on position within company? 
2. What specific activities are included in your organization's onboarding plan (e.g., orientation sessions, training modules)? Do these differ depending upon employee rank/position level of person being hired for same role across different departments at the time that they start working with us or not and why is this done?
3. How long does it typically take from an individual's first day until he / she feels comfortable in their new position, both professionally as well socially within team environment if possible provide statistics related to turnover rate after one year of employment based on whether they went through formalized process or not and why do you think this happens?
4. How does your company measure the effectiveness/success ratio for its employee orientation program (e.g., surveys, evaluations from new hires themselves)? Is there a way to quantify impact felt by those who have underwent onboarding versus others that did not and why is it important if you could share?
5. What are some common challenges faced during the first few weeks of employment for newly hired individuals (either internal or external factors) which can be improved with better communication, training materials etc., so they feel more prepared to perform their job successfully from day one onwards and not struggle too much in beginning period due lack knowledge about company culture & values?
6. Is there a mentorship system available within your organization where experienced employees guide newcomers through transition process making sure all necessary steps taken care off including paperwork, technology setup etc., before they begin working officially or no such thing exists and if not why is that so despite its numerous benefits seen at other places?
7. How does management team ensure onboarding program stays current with changing times as far business practices go (either legal requirements alter over time OR simply new methods adopted by industry leaders) making certain our workforce remains competitive while still being able to adapt quickly when need arises without causing undue stress or confusion among staff members who might be accustomed older ways of doing things?
8. Can you please share any specific success stories related directly with successful onboarding process, perhaps even mention how many people were positively impacted by these changes and what was their role within company after being integrated properly into workforce environment without much hassle or resistance faced from others due to good planning ahead of time?
9. Finally - if there is anything else you'd like us (the user)to know about your onboarding process, please feel free share here in open-ended format; we are always eager learn and improve based off feedback received! Thank You!!

2. Do you think the manager communicates effectively with team members and other managers within our organization, on a scale of 1 to 5? (Multiple choice) A- Strongly agree B – Agree c - Neutral D - Disagree e -Strongly disagree F - Prefer not to say
3. How often does your manager provide feedback about performance and growth opportunities for team members, on a scale of one to five ? 1 being never ,5 Being always? (Multiple choice) A- Strongly agree B – Agre c - Neutral D - Disagree e -Strongly disagree F
4. Is the supervisor open minded about new ideas and suggestions from team members, on a scale of one to five ? 1 being never ,5 Being always? (Multiple choice) A- Strongly agree B – Agre c - Neutral D - Disagree e -Strongly disagree F
5. Is the manager able to motivate their employees and create an engaging work environment, on a scale of one to five ? 1 being never ,5 Being always? (Multiple choice) A- Strongly agree B – Agre c - Neutral D - Disagree e -Strongly disagree F
6. How well does the manager handle conflict within their team and mediate disputes, on a scale of one to five ? 1 being never ,5 Being always? (Multiple choice) A- Strongly agree B – Agre c - Neutral D - Disagree e -Strongly disagree F
7. Is your supervisor able to create an environment that encourages team members and fosters a sense of community, on a scale from 1 being never ,5 Being always? (Multiple choice) A- Strongly agree B – Agre c - Neutral D - Disagree e -Strongly disagree F
8. Do you feel like your manager is able to create an environment that encourages innovation and creativity, on a scale of one to five ? 1 being never ,5 Being always? (Multiple choice) A- Strongly agree B – Agre c - Neutral D - Disagree e -Strongly disagree F

10. Do you feel like your manager is able to create an environment that encourages a good work life balance, on a scale of one to five ? 1 being never ,5 Being always? (Multiple choice) A- Strongly agree B – Agre c - Neutral D - Disagree e

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a potential questionnaire about career paths:
1. How would you describe your current role at work? (e.g., job title, level)
2. Do you feel like there are clear opportunities for advancement in the company or within your specific department? If so, can you name any positions that seem to be a natural progression from where you currently stand professionally?
3. Have you ever had access to an official list of job titles and their corresponding salary ranges at our organization (or one similar enough) for purposes such as career development planning or succession management/planning, etcetera ? If not what would be the best way in your opinion that this information should reach employees?
4. Do you feel like there are certain skills required to move up within a company and if so which ones do think those might include (either technical abilities related directly with job or soft-skills)? 5 How long have been working for our organization, how many people in your department/team can recall having seen promoted?
6. Do you feel like there is enough information available about the career paths of employees who had similar jobs as yours and were able to progress within company ? If not what would be best way this info should reach all staff members interested for example by creating a wiki page or something else that could help people understand better how they can grow professionally.
7 Do you feel encouraged enough at work, do your supervisors provide regular feedback about performance and if yes is there any constructive criticism provided to improve? 8 How many employees in the company are aware of their career paths within organization or have a clear plan for professional growth ? If not what would be best way this information should reach all staff members interested.
9 Do you feel that your current role aligns with long-term goals and aspirations, if so can name any specific tasks responsibilities which make it seem like perfect fit? 10 How often do supervisors discuss career development plans or opportunities for advancement during performance evaluations ? If not what would be best way to introduce this topic in organization.
Please let me know whether you need help with anything else!

```vbnet
5) How does management measure whether a particular employee has been trained effectively in their role, if at all. Is there any formal process for measuring the success of training programs currently implemented within your organization and how could these be improved? Please provide examples!  
6) What do you think about using technology platforms such as virtual reality to deliver immersive learning experiences rather than traditional classroom settings or self-paced online classes (Strongly Agree, Somewhat agree/disagree)? 	Please explain your answer.   
7) How important is it for employees in this organization that they receive regular training and education on topics related directly to their job responsibilities? Please rate from a scale of one through ten!  
8 ) Do you think the company provides enough opportunities or resources available so staff can further educate themselves outside work hours, such as paid courses/certifications etc. (Yes / No)? If not what would make it better and why do they feel this way? 	Please provide examples if possible!!   
9) How many times have you personally been sent on an external training course in the past year for your job role or responsibilities, please rate from a scale of one through ten. (Never/1-2 Times / More than twice per annum). Please explain why this number is what it has turned out to be!
```

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a set of questions related to learner feedback for a specific course:
1) On a scale from 1-5, how would you rate the overall quality and usefulness of this course? Please provide your rating.
2) Were there any aspects or parts of the course that stood out as particularly engaging/useful? If so, which ones were they? And why do YOU think those particular elements worked well for you? (This will help us understand what works best!)
3) In terms of content and delivery style: Did this specific training meet your expectations in these areas or not – please explain. We’re also interested to know whether the pace was right, too fast/slow etc., so let's hear it! 😊
4) How about interaction with other learners? Was there enough time allocated for group work and discussions during this course session - if yes then great but just in case please share your thoughts. If not – what would have made the difference here?! And how did you feel when working alone or as part of a team within that training environment ?
5) Do YOU think our assessment methods accurately reflect learner performance? We'd be grateful for any specific comments on this topic, including whether certain types and levels should perhaps get more attention. 🤓 In addition: Is there anything you would like to see changed in the way we measure success or progress through tests/exams etc., going forward ?
6) How did YOU feel about technology use throughout your course? Were all necessary tools provided, including software updates and technical support if required – let us know! And how can this aspect be improved for future learners' benefit. 🙏 In fact: Do you have any tech-related suggestions at ALL that would help our next generation of students thrive in their educational journeys ?
7) Finally - the big one : Based on your experience with THIS course, what changes or improvements do YOU feel need to be made before it can become a truly stellar learning environment? We're all ears and value every single opinion here! 😊🙏 Thank you very much for taking part in this questionnaire.
Please note: All responses will remain confidential unless otherwise stated by the participant themselves, allowing us valuable insights into our training programs without causing any discomfort or harm to those involved - hooray !

This is a JSON representation of an employee experience questionnaire. It includes 7 questions with the following details:

1. "How satisfied are you with your current role?" - 5-point Likert scale
2. "Do you feel that the company values its employees as individuals or just sees them as a necessary resource to achieve business goals?" - Yes/No
3. "How often do you feel comfortable sharing your thoughts and opinions with your colleagues, even if they are not in line with company culture/policy?" - 5-point Likert scale
4. "Do you feel that the company provides adequate resources for professional growth?" - Yes/No
5. "How many training sessions have you attended in last 6 months?" - Number
6. "How often do your personal values align with those of the organization?" - 5-point Likert scale
7. "Do you feel that the company's policies are fair?" - Yes/No

Each question is assigned a unique code, and the order in which it should be displayed is specified through the "DISPLAY\_ORDER" property. The "TYPE\_ID" property indicates the type of answer for that question, for example, a Likert scale, Yes/No, or number. The "ANSWER" property specifies the actual answer given by the respondent.

-------------------
[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100003
     - Topic: Access to Technology and Tools
     - Question number: 10
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator that helps HR users investigate phenomena within the company.
Firstly, the user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic.
Then, the user will ask to convert it into a specified format.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. 

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Access to Technology and Tools

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a potential questionnaire for access to technology and tools:
1. How would you rate your overall level of comfort with using various technologies in both personal and professional settings? Please use the following scale: Very Comfortable, Somewhat Comcomforteble, or Not at All Comfortable. If not comfortable, please specify which specific techologies make it difficult for you to feel confident while interacting/using them (if known).
2. How often do your technology needs change? Please use the following scale: Constantly Changing Environment / Frequently changing environment - 30 days or less than a month; Occasionally- every few months, but not more frequent then that and Rarely once in several years/Never (if known).
3. Have you ever felt like your technology tools are outdated? Please use the following scale: Yes / No if yes please specify which technologies do feel old or need an upgrade to make it work better for me as a user(If Known) and reason behind that feeling of obsolescence (if known).
4. Do you think there is enough training provided on how technology tools should be used? Please use the following scale: Yes / No if no please specify what kind/type or amount would make it better for me as a user(If Known) and why do not feel that way about this (if known).
5. Do you think your current level of access to various technology tools is sufficient, too much or insufficient? Please use the following scale: Sufficent / Too Much/Not Enough if Not enough please specify what kind(type)/how many and why do not feel that way about this (if known).
6. Do you think your current level of access to various technology tools is sufficient, too much or insufficient? Please use the following scale: Sufficent / Too Much/Not Enough if Not enough please specify what kind(type)/how many and why do not feel that way about this (if known).

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a potential questionnaire on access to technology and tools:
1. How would you rate your overall level of comfort with using various technologies, such as computers, smartphones, tablets, etc., in the workplace? (Please use a scale from 0-5 where zero indicates no experience at all.) Can you please specify what makes this number so low or high for you personally and which technology do not feel comfortable to work around.
2. Have your managers/supervisors ever discussed with you about using certain technologies that are considered outdated? If yes, how did it make you felt when they mentioned those tools as a suggestion in place of the ones currently being used by team members who have more experience than yourself and why do not feel comfortable to use them.
3. Do your current technology resources allow for effective collaboration with colleagues within or outside organization (please specify)? If no, what specific limitations are preventing you from collaborating effectively? And how can those be overcome in order make sure everyone has access same tools regardless of their location and role inside company structure hierarchy systematically not just when it comes to special cases.
4. How often do your technology resources fail or become unavailable due either software updates, hardware failures/malfunctions etc., causing disruptions at work? Please share any specific incidents where this has happened recently if possible along with their impact on productivity and communication between team members during those times when things were not working properly
5. Have you ever been prevented from using a certain technology resource because of cost constraints or budgetary reasons, even though it would have made your job easier? If yes can please share how did this make an impression in terms both short term (easy to overcome) and long-term implications for yourself as well others around who might need those same resources too.
6. In general do you feel that the technology tools provided by company are up-to date with industry standards or not? Can please elaborate on reasons behind this answer, including any personal experiences which have led one to think in such a way about current state of affairs when it comes down accessing necessary materials required for doing job well.
7. How frequently do you receive training opportunities related specifically towards new technologies and tools within company setting rather than general self-improvement sessions? And how important is this type learning experience compared other types which could be made available instead, such as team building activities or problem solving workshops etc., when it comes to improving overall performance of workforce.
8. Are there any specific technology resources that would help you perform better at your job if only they were more readily accessible? If yes can please list them along with reasons why these particular items are important in order make sure everyone has access same tools regardless their location and role inside company structure hierarchy systematically not just when it comes to special cases.
9. Finally, do the technology resources provided by your organization take into account different abilities of employees? For example: Are there options for those who may have visual or hearing impairments; physical disabilities etc., making sure everyone can use materials without any issues arising due lack proper consideration given beforehand during design process
Thank you very much!

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a potential career development questionnaire:

1. How do you define "career development"? Is it something that happens naturally, or does it require intentional effort?
2. What specific steps have you taken to further your own career development and advancement within the company? Can you share some examples of things you've done proactively rather than waiting for them to happen organically?
3. How do you assess whether a particular opportunity or experience is valuable in terms of professional growth, versus something that might be considered "dead-end"? Are there certain criteria you use when making this determination about what will help your career progression and which things are not as important/useful to have on resume?
4. How do you feel about mentoring others who may want guidance in their own careers from someone with more experience than they currently possess themselves - whether formal or informal arrangements, including shadowing etcetera ? Do think this is an effective way of sharing knowledge and skills between people within organization so everyone can benefit mutually?
5. In terms career development do you believe that certain roles offer greater potential for growth compared to others due their inherent nature being more strategic/higher up on organizational chart, or does it depend solely upon individual's personal drive & ambition regardless of position they hold currently ? Please elaborate if possible !
6. What role has feedback played in your own career development - both giving and receiving? Do you agree with statement that "feedback is food for growth"? If yes then how do ensure people are receptive to hearing it, not defensive or dismissing outright due its potential discomfort associated w criticism ? 
7. How important has networking been in your own career journey - both internal and external networks? Can you share any anecdotes about times when having strong network helped propel forward into new role/opportunity that might have otherwise passed by unnoticed, or instances where not being well connected held back progress ?
8. How do organizations balance need for promoting from within versus bringing in fresh perspectives through external hires? Is there a sweet spot between these two approaches which allows best of both worlds while minimizing any potential downsides associated with either approach - such as disgruntlement among existing workforce or lackluster performance by newcomers who aren't given chance to prove themselves properly ?
9. How can one measure success when it comes career development, especially if they are not in a traditional leadership role but still feel fulfilled and contributing positively through other means? Are there certain metrics that should be applied universally or does this differ from person-to-person based on their unique circumstances & goals ?
10. Finally - what advice would you give someone looking to further own career development, whether they're just starting out in workforce and trying figure things quickly OR experienced professional seeking next step up ladder? Is there anything specific that comes mind as crucial for success beyond general ideas like hardwork/dedication etcetera ?
Please let me know if I can help with any additional questions or information!

[LLM ANSWER] -> JSON 
 Here is the questionnaire in JSON format, as requested:

```json
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "CAREER_DEVELOPMENT",
        "NAME": "Career Development Questionnaire",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "CAREER_DEVELOPMENT_Q1",
            "NAME": "What specific steps have you taken to further your own career development and advancement within the company?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "I have taken several steps to further my career development, including pursuing additional education and training, seeking out mentors, and volunteering for high-visibility projects."
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "I have not taken any specific steps to further my career development. I believe that opportunities will come to me naturally as I perform my current job well."
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "I have taken some steps to further my career development, but I am still evaluating what else I can do to progress further."
              }
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "CAREER_DEVELOPMENT_Q2",
            "NAME": "How do you assess whether a particular opportunity or experience is valuable in terms of professional growth, versus something that might be considered 'dead-end'?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "I assess opportunities and experiences based on whether they will help me learn new skills, meet new people, and gain more responsibility. If an opportunity does not meet these criteria, I would consider it less valuable."
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "I assess opportunities and experiences based on whether they align with my personal values and goals. If an opportunity does not match my values and goals, I would consider it less valuable."
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "I assess opportunities and experiences based on whether they will provide me with a better work-life balance. If an opportunity does not offer better work-life balance, I would consider it less valuable."
              }
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "CAREER_DEVELOPMENT_Q3",
            "NAME": "How important has networking been in your own career journey - both internal and external networks?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "Networking has been extremely important in my career journey. I have built strong relationships with people who can help me find new opportunities and learn from their experiences."
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Networking has been somewhat important in my career journey. I have built some relationships with people who can help me find new opportunities and learn from their experiences."
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Networking has not been important in my career journey. I believe that performance in a job is more important than who you know."
              }
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

This questionnaire includes three questions about career development, with each question allowing the respondent to choose multiple answers. The questions ask about specific steps taken for career development, how opportunities are assessed, and the importance of networking. The answers are rated on a scale of 1 to 5, with 1 being not important and 5 being extremely important.

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100011
     - Topic: Career Path Clarity
     - Question number: 9
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator that helps HR users investigate phenomena within the company.
Firstly, the user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic.
Then, the user will ask to convert it into a specified format.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. 

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Career Path Clarity

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a potential questionnaire for investigating career path clarity within an organization:
1) How would you describe the level of transparency around different job roles in this company? Is it easy to understand how they fit into broader organizational goals and what skills are required at each stage?
2) Do employees feel that there is a clear progression from one role or career pathway to another, with defined steps for growth within their current position as well as future opportunities? Or do people tend to stay in the same job level without any promotion opportunity due to lack of clarity about what's next step and how it can be achieved.
3) Is there a system that allows employees at all levels access information they need regarding potential career paths, including resources such as training programs or mentorship opportunities? Or do people have to search for this info themselves which may lead them feeling unsupported by management team when trying reach next level in their careers . 4. Are current managers encouraged and supported through specific initiatives (either internal trainings/workshops) about leading teams effectively, so they can help employees understand how best perform tasks necessary not only within the context of job but also as part broader organizational goals?
5. How often do you think people should be reviewed for potential promotion or reassignment based on performance and skills acquired over time rather than just being given a certain number years before moving up automatically without considering individual circumstances - this could help ensure everyone has equal chance at growth regardless of background noise like personal life events affecting progression speed negatively.
6) Is there any kind program/initiative in place where employees can give feedback about their managers, supervisors and leaders directly which then used by management team to make decisions around promotions or other personnel actions? This would help ensure those who are best suited for leadership roles get recognized while also providing an outlet for constructive criticism from staff members.
7) Finally - do you feel like there's a strong connection between personal growth and professional development within this organization, where people encouraged not only to learn new skills but apply them in practice through projects or initiatives which could lead both individual success AND organizational benefits? If yes then what specific practices/programmes exist making it happen.
Please let me know if you would like any modifications made before I send out these questions!

     - System:

Generate me a questionnaire on Employee Potential

-------------------

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure thing! Here is a potential questionnaire for investigating employee potential:

2. In your opinion, what are some benefits and drawbacks associated with giving both positive and negative feedback in the workplace? Please provide specific examples if possible!
3. Which communication channels have been used for providing/receiving constructive criticism within our company so far - email, face-to-face conversation or something else entirely? Could you please rank them based on their effectiveness from your perspective as an HR representative of this organization and share why do think that way about those methods being more effective than others.
4. How can we ensure all employees feel comfortable giving AND receiving feedback without any fear, pressure or judgment attached to it - especially when dealing with sensitive topics like personal growth/development area etc? Please elaborate on your thoughts regarding this matter!
5. What steps should be taken if someone feels they are being unfairly criticized through our current system and believe the criticism is unjustified; how can we help them address those concerns while maintaining confidentiality for both parties involved in process of giving/receiving feedback? Can you please share some ideas about this situation from your experience as an HR professional working at similar organization like ours.
6. Is there a designated time frame within which people should provide their thoughts and opinions regarding performance, or is it more important to have ongoing dialogue throughout the year - if so then how can we encourage such conversations without making them feel burdensome for everyone involved in process of giving/receiving feedback? Please share your insights concerning this matter.
7. How do you think technology could be leveraged further within our organization when it comes to providing and receiving better quality, more actionable performance-related comments - especially given the rise of AI tools available today that can potentially help automate some aspects but still keep human touch alive in communication process? Can we have your expert opinion about this subject.
8. Finally, do you feel our current feedback mechanism encourages growth and development among team members or rather just serves as a tool for pointing out mistakes without any clear path towards improvement - please share detailed explanation based on data collected from similar organizations if possible! Thank You!"

     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator that helps HR users investigate phenomena within the company.
Firstly, the user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic.
Then, the user will ask to convert it into a specified format.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Internal Mobility Opportunities

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure thing! Here is a potential questionnaire for investigating internal mobility opportunities within a company:

1. How would you describe the current state of internal mobility at our organization? Is it easy or difficult to move from one department to another, and why?
2. Do employees feel encouraged to explore new roles in different parts of the company, even if those positions are not directly related to their previous job responsibilities? If so, what specific actions does management take to promote internal mobility?
3. How do we currently measure or track our progress on promoting a culture that supports and encourages movement between departments/roles within the organization? Are there any metrics in place for this purpose yet?
4. What are some of the biggest obstacles preventing employees from moving around internally, if you feel they exist at all? Is it due to lack of resources or something else entirely? And how can we address those issues effectively as a team and company-wide initiative so everyone has equal opportunity for growth regardless their location/department preference.
5a) In your opinion: Should there be any kind of formal training program available within the organization, which would help employees learn new skills necessary to perform different jobs across departments? If yes – what topics should this education cover and how often it needs updating based on industry trends & technology advancements; 	and  
5b) How can we make sure that all staff members have access not just technically but also physically (if needed through remote learning platforms or other means), so they don't miss out because of geographical location.   
6a). Is there a clear career path defined for each role within the company? If yes, how does management communicate this information to their team and ensure everyone understands it clearly; 	and  
6b) How can we make sure that every employee has access not just theoretically but also practically (if needed through mentoring programs or other means), so they don't miss out because of lack of support/guidance.   
7a). Do you think our organization provides enough opportunities for employees to learn about different roles and departments, especially those which are less known? If not – how can we increase awareness among staff members regarding all the possibilities within their reach; 	and  
7b) How do YOU make sure that everyone has equal chance of getting familiar with various aspects regardless if they're introverted or extrovert type people.   
8a). Is there a process in place for employees to apply internally when positions become available? If yes – how does management ensure this is communicated effectively and timely, so all interested parties have equal chance of applying; 	and  
8b) How can we make sure that every employee has access not just technically but also practically (if needed through technology platforms or other means), to the job application system.   
9a). Do you think our organization's internal mobility policies are fair and unbiased? If yes, how do YOU ensure this is true across all departments/locations; 	and  
9b) How can we make sure that everyone has equal chance of being considered for a new role regardless their background or personal preferences.   
10a). Is there any kind of onboarding process available within the organization, which would help employees integrate into different roles and departments? If yes – how does management ensure this is effective across all areas; 	and  
10b) How can we make sure that every employee has access not just technically but also practically (if needed through technology platforms or other means), to onboarding resources.   
Please let me know if there are any additional questions you would like added!
     - User:

Generate me a questionnaire on Internal Mobility Opportunities

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a potential questionnaire for investigating internal mobility opportunities within a company:

1. How would you describe the current state of internal mobility at our organization? Is it easy or difficult to move from one department to another, and why do you think that is?
2. Do we have any formal programs in place designed specifically to encourage employees' growth through different positions inside the company? If so, could you please list them along with their goals/objectives for each program? And if not - what would be needed (resources or otherwise)to make this happen and how many people are estimated required
3. Are there any specific skills that we look at when considering someone to fill a higher-level position internally, rather than hiring from outside the company? If yes then please specify those skill sets/qualities as well what is your opinion about them being mandatory for internal candidates or not ? And if no - why do you think this might be and how can we improve it
4. How would an employee go about finding out that there are new opportunities available within the company? Is our current communication system effective in letting people know of these chances to grow, both horizontally as well vertically inside organization ? If not then what could/should change so employees feel more informed and empowered when it comes time for them move up or sideways
5. Do you think that internal mobility is a good thing? Why do we want our people growing through different positions instead of just staying in one place, possibly becoming stagnant overtime ? If yes then how can this be encouraged further within the company and if no - why not so what could change to make it more appealing for employees
6. Are there any specific challenges that you see with internal mobility? How do we overcome them as a team or individually in order get people moving around comfortably inside our organization ? If yes then please specify those challenge(s) along the ways they can be tackled and how many resources are required to make it happen
7. Do different departments have their own specific requirements for internal mobility? Are there any that might not want someone from another department joining them because of certain prerequisites or qualifications needed ? If yes then what could change so everyone feels welcome regardless where they come in the company and how many resources are required to make it happen
8. How do we measure success when an employee moves internally? Is there any specific metrics that you use, such as time spent on task before moving vs after or some other method of evaluation ? If not then what would be needed (resources/tools)to establish this kind measurement system and how many people are estimated required to make it happen
9. Can we say for sure if internal mobility is a cost-effective solution? Are there any hidden costs associated with having employees move around internally, such as training time or other resources ? If yes then what could change so that moving someone from one place in the company doesn't feel like an extra burden on finances and how many people are estimated required to make it happen
10. Finally - do you think internal mobility is a good thing? Why should we encourage our employees growing through different positions instead of just staying put, possibly becoming stagnant overtime ? If yes then what could change so that everyone feels encouraged about this opportunity and if no – why not

Generate me a questionnaire on Job Satisfaction

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! I can help you create a job satisfaction survey with engaging and thought-provoking questions that provide valuable insights about employee happiness, motivation, and productivity in their roles within the company:
```vbnet
1) How often do your values align with those of this organization? (Strongly Disagree to Strongly Agree scale.) 	(Text format - TFFF question type for use as a filter/exclusion criteria).  
2a. Do you feel that the work assigned is meaningful and has purpose, or just something else on your plate with no real meaning? (Yes / No)    (Multiple choice questions to keep things simple.) 	(Text format - TFFF question type for use as a filter/exclusion criteria).
3b. How often do you feel that the work assigned is meaningful and has purpose, or just something else on your plate with no real meaning?  0=Never;1-2 times per month ;48  =Every day (Likert scale)   	(Text format - TFFF question type for use as a filter/exclusion criteria).
```
Here is the list of questions in text and multiple choice formats:
Questions to ask employees about job satisfaction, with an explanation after each one. Please note that these are just suggestions; you can modify them or add more based on your specific needs! The TFFF format means True/False-True/ False for use as a filtering question in the analysis stage of this survey:
1) How often do your values align with those of this organization? (Strongly Disagree to Strongly Agree scale.) 	(Text format - TFFF question type). This is an excellent way to understand if someone feels connected and engaged at work. It can help identify any disconnects between personal beliefs/values vs company culture, which could be affecting job satisfaction negatively!
2a) Do you feel that the tasks assigned are meaningful or just something else on your plate with no real meaning? (Yes / No). 	(Multiple choice questions to keep things simple.) This question is essential because it can help determine if someone feels like their work has a purpose and they're not simply doing 'busy-work.'
3b) How often do you feel that the tasks assigned are meaningful or just something else on your plate with no real meaning? 0=Never;1-2 times per month ;48 =Every day. (Likert scale). This question is a more detailed version of number two and will help us understand how frequently people experience this feeling, which can then be used to create strategies for making work feel meaningful!
```vbnet
Question 3: "How often do you have the opportunity at your job or in meetings with management/colleagues where everyone is heard equally?" (0=Never;1-2 times per month ;48 =Every day)   	(Text format - Likert scale question type).   This will help determine if people feel empowered and able to contribute their thoughts, which can be an essential factor in job satisfaction.
```
Question 3: "How often do you have the opportunity at your job or in meetings with management/colleagues where everyone is heard equally?" (0=Never;1-2 times per month ;48 =Every day)	(Text format - Likert scale question type). This will help determine if people feel empowered and able to contribute their thoughts, which can be an essential factor in job satisfaction.
```vbnet
Question 3: "How often do you have the opportunity at your job or in meetings with management/colleagues where everyone is heard equally?" (0=Never;1-2 times per month ;48 =Every day)   	(Text format - Likert scale question type).   This will help determine if people feel empowered and able to contribute their thoughts, which can be an essential factor in job satisfaction.
```

Generate me a questionnaire on Job Satisfaction

[LLM ANSWER] -> JSON 
 Here is the JSON format of the questionnaire on Job Satisfaction:
```json
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "JS",
        "NAME": "Job Satisfaction",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "JS_Q1",
            "NAME": "How often do your values align with those of this organization?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "Strongly Disagree"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Disagree"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Neutral"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Agree"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Strongly Agree"
              }
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "JS_Q2",
            "NAME": "Do you feel that the tasks assigned are meaningful or just something else on your plate with no real meaning?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "Yes"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "No"
              }
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "JS_Q3",
            "NAME": "How often do you feel that the tasks assigned are meaningful or just something else on your plate with no real meaning?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "0=Never"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "1-2 times per month"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "48"
              }
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```
This JSON format contains the same questions as the text format, but in a more structured and organized way. The 'CODE' and 'NAME' properties are used to identify each question, while the 'DISPLAY_ORDER' property is used to order the questions in a specific way. The 'TYPE\_ID' property is used to determine the type of question, and the '_TF\_ANSWERS' array contains all the possible answers for each question.


```vbnet
7) How was the venue of meeting? Was it easy to move around, hear everyone clearly without any disturbance. If you could change anything about this part what would that be?! And how did THAT make YOU feel! :)  5 being very good and zero not at all  !!   4 is average !!!
```
1. How was the facilitator of meeting? Were they able to keep everyone engaged, motivated throughout session or you felt like it could have been better ? If yes then what made that person so great?! And how did THAT make YOU feel! :)  5 being very good and zero not at all  !!   4 is average
2. How was the food provided? Was there enough for everybody with variety too, if no please specify who didn't get any or felt left out in this section !!!!!! :( And how did that make YOU feel! :)  5 being very good and zero not at all  !!   4 is average

This JSON object contains a single questionnaire with 4 questions. The first question is a rating question, the second and third questions are selection questions, and the fourth question is a number question. The `DISPLAY_ORDER` property is used to order the questions. The `ANSWER` property for the rating questions is a number between 1 and 5, and for selection questions it is the number of selected options.

 Sure! Here is a potential questionnaire for investigating leadership effectiveness:

1. To what extent do you agree that our organizational leaders clearly communicate their vision, goals, and expectations?
2. How often have you observed instances of favoritism or bias in decision-making by the leader(s)? If yes, how frequently is this happening?
3. Do you feel encouraged to share your thoughts about work processes with leadership team members without fearing negative consequences such as being ignored/overruled because they are not part of “in” group (either due to rank or personal relationships) ? 4- How often do leaders use data and facts when making decisions?
5. In a scale from one(lowest level )to ten how would you rate the ability for our leadership team in understanding their audience’s needs, wants ,and preferences before delivering any message/information to them (either internal or external) ? 6- Do they use different communication styles depending on whether it is an employee versus a client?
7. How often do leaders take time out of your day and ask for feedback about how things are going in the organization, not just when there’s some big problem that needs fixing right away (either through one to ones or other methods)? 8- Do you think our leadership team is able enough with managing conflicts among employees?
9. How often do leaders make an effort and try new ways of doing things instead always relying on same old techniques, even if they’re not working well anymore ? (either through one to ones or other methods) 10- In a scale from zero(lowest level )to ten how would you rate the ability for our leadership team in creating an environment where people are encouraged and empowered rather than feeling controlled by management?

10 . Does your current supervisor create an environment in which team members are motivated and engaged ?(Never , Rarely, Sometimes Most Of The Time or Always ) 11. How often do you feel that this leader is able to understand the needs of their employees? ( Never Fewer than once a month Once A Week Or More Than One week)

1. To what extent do you agree that our current leaders have clear values, principles, or beliefs about how things should be done? (Strongly disagree to strongly agree)
2. How often does your leader demonstrate behaviors and actions consistent with their stated vision/values in a given week? Never / Rarely / Sometimes / Most of the time / Always
3. To what extent do you feel that our leaders are able to inspire others within the organization through effective communication, motivation techniques etc (Strongly disagree - Strongly agree)
4. How often does your leader demonstrate behaviors and actions consistent with their vision/values in a given week? Never / Rarely / Sometimes / Most of the time / Always
5. To what extent do you feel that our leaders are able to create an environment where people can speak up about issues or concerns without fear (Strongly disagree - Strongly agree)
6. How often does your leader demonstrate behaviors and actions consistent with creating a psychologically safe work climate in which team members actively help each other? Never / Rarely/ Sometimes / Most of the time / Always 7. To what extent do you feel that our leaders are able to create an environment where people can speak up about issues or concerns without fear (Strongly disagree - Strongly agree)
8. How often does your leader demonstrate behaviors and actions consistent with creating a positive work climate? Never/ Rarely / Sometimes / Most of the time / Always 9. To what extent do you feel that our leaders are able to create an environment where people can speak up about issues or concerns without fear (Strongly disagree - Strongly agree)
10. How often does your leader demonstrate behaviors and actions consistent with creating a positive work climate? Never/ Rarely / Sometimes / Most of the time / Always 11. To what extent do you feel that our leaders are able to create an environment where people can speak up about issues or concerns without fear (Strongly disagree - Strongly agree)

8. Can you share some success stories about individuals who have gone through your training programs and seen positive changes in terms of skill sets, productivity levels or overall job satisfaction since then 🤓 ? 9. What are some common barriers preventing employees from taking advantage offered training opportunities inside your organization, such as time constraints or lack of motivation 🤓 ? Have you considered offering incentives like bonuses/raises if people complete required number hours related coursework within specific period timeline before being granted certain level certification stating they meet standards expected by company?
10. Finally - how do your training programs cater to different learning styles, such as visual learners or those who prefer hands-on activities over listening passively during lecture 🤓 ? Are there any plans in place for making sure everyone can access materials needed regardless preferred method absorbing information without feeling overwhelmed by sheer volume content presented all at once?

```json
                "ANSWER": "Never"
              }
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

This questionnaire has six questions. The first question is a rating question about overall satisfaction with the training and development programs. The second question is a frequency question about how often the participant takes part in training and development programs. The third question is a multiple choice question about the participant's preferred method of receiving training and development materials. The fourth question is a rating question about the effectiveness of the training and development programs. The fifth question is a multiple choice question about the participant's preferred method of receiving training and development materials. The sixth question is a frequency question about how often the participant feels like they need additional training and development in their current role.

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here's a set of engaging and thought-provoking questions about worklife balance:

1. How would you rate your overall level of job satisfaction, using a scale from 0 (completely unsatisfied) to 5 (extremely satisfied)? Please also share what factors contribute the most towards this number.
2. Do you feel that there is enough separation between work and personal life? If not, which areas need improvement in your opinion?
3. How often do tasks from home or other non-work related activities creep into professional time (either at office hours or during weekends)? Please share the frequency of this occurrence on a scale: 0 - Never; 1 to 5 – Occasionally, but not disruptive and with no negative consequences.
4. In terms of workload distribution throughout your day/week, do you feel that there is enough time for both professional tasks as well personal activities? Please share the frequency on a scale: 0 - Never; 1 to 5 – Occasionally (but still not disruptive and with no negative consequences).
5. How often are work-related thoughts or concerns present in your mind during nonwork hours, such that you can’t fully disconnect? Please share the frequency on a scale: 0 - Never; 1 to 3 – Occasionally (but still not disruptive and with no negative consequences).
6. Have any of these work-life balance factors ever caused tension or conflict in your personal relationships, such as family members wanting more time together? Please share the frequency on a scale: Yes/No - Frequency out of 10 is also acceptable (e.g., "Yes" with an average score from colleagues).
7. Have you considered changing jobs because work-life balance was not met in your current role, or do other factors play more important roles? Please share the frequency on a scale: Yes/No - Frequency out of 10 is also acceptable (e.g., "Yes" with an average score from colleagues).
8. How often are you able to take time off work for self-care activities, such as exercise or hobbies that help maintain your overall health and wellbeing? Please share the frequency on a scale: 1 - Never; 2 – Rarely (but still not disruptive); upwards of here with no negative consequences.
9. How often do you feel like work-related stresses are affecting other aspects in life, such as sleep or appetite patterns and overall health? Please share the frequency on a scale: Yes/No - Frequency out of 10 is also acceptable (e.g., "Yes" with an average score from colleagues).
10. Finally – if there was one thing you could change about your work-life balance, what would that be and why? Please share the frequency on a scale: Yes/No - Frequency out of 5 for importance is also acceptable (e.g., "Yes" with an average score from colleagues).
Please let me know if there's anything else I can do to help!

 Sure thing! Here is a potential questionnaire on workload management:

1. How do you currently prioritize tasks at work? Is there a system in place, or are they taken as they come?
2. Have you ever felt overwhelmed by the number of projects and responsibilities assigned to you within your role? If so, how did this affect your performance?
3. Do you think that current methods for managing workload effectively allocate time between tasks based on priority level? Or do certain types or levels seem more prone to causing stress than others?
4. How often have adjustments been made in terms of timelines and resources when a task is deemed too difficult due solely because its associated with an unrealistic deadline rather than actual ability required for completion ? 5 Is there any formality around requesting additional support or time if needed, such as through management approval?
6. To what extent do you feel that your workload affects others in the organization and their productivity too - either positively (because they can learn from watching how someone else manages) negatively because it spills over into other areas unintentionally ? 7 How frequently are team members asked to help eachother out with tasks, versus being given new projects independently?
8. Is there a clear understanding of what constitutes an 'acceptable' workload for your role and others within the company - or is it more fluid depending on situation/project needs at any one time ? 9 Can you identify specific times during day when most productive / least stressed, versus periods where feel overwhelmed by demands placed upon?
10. How regularly do people consider taking some form of workload management training to better cope with high pressure situations and multiple tasks requiring attention simultaneously - either self-taught or through external providers ? 11 Finally: if given choice between two similar but slightly different projects, how would you decide which one takes priority?

 Sure! Here is a potential questionnaire on workload management:

1. How do you currently manage your daily tasks, chores, or responsibilities? Is there a specific system in place that helps prioritize and balance these activities to avoid feeling overwhelmed by the sheer volume of things-to-do (workload)? If yes, can we please elaborate on this method/system for better understanding.
2. Do you feel comfortable with your current work schedule or do you think it could be improved? Please explain why if so! 3. Do certain activities take up most or all your attention while others are left unattended? If yes, how do you ensure that these critical few get completed and not at the expense of other tasks which might be equally important in a different context! Is there an automatic system to help distribute time slots for each task based on their priority level.
4. How often does your workload change throughout one week or month? And what measures are taken, if any; when it comes down from peak levels and vice versa during these fluctuations so that productivity remains constant despite varying amounts of tasks at hand! Can we please elaborate more about this mechanism for better understanding how things flow smoothly without interruptions.
5. Have you ever felt like certain activities should not be part of your workload? If yes, why did they end up there in the first place and what steps were taken to remove them from being a burden on yourself or others around! A simple technique for identifying non-essential tasks early can help prevent future occurrences.
6. How do you handle unexpected situations that pop into your workload without warning? Are these handled well, considering they weren't planned initially but still need attention now more than ever before because of their urgency and importance attached to them suddenly! Can we please elaborate on this technique for better understanding how such sudden tasks are managed.
7. Is there a way or tool that could help manage your workload? Something like an application, software program, physical planner/organizer - anything which has been found useful by others too in managing their own set of responsibilities and activities! Please share if any so we can explore its feasibility within our system as well.
8. How do you measure the success or failure rate when it comes to workload management? Is there a metric, key performance indicator (KPI), which tells us whether things are going smoothly OR NOT - this is important because without knowing how good/bad we're doing; no corrective action can be taken if required.
9. Finally, do you think your current methods for managing workload could use some updating or modernization? If yes again why and what changes would make it better suited to today’s fast-paced working environment! The answer might help us all improve our time management skills significantly by adopting new practices in place of old ones.
10. And finally, do you have any advice for others who struggle with workload just like yourself? Something simple yet effective which has worked wonders over the years and can be shared here too! This question will help us build a supportive community around this topic so everyone feels comfortable sharing their thoughts openly without fear of judgment or criticism.

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a potential questionnaire about workplace culture:

1. How would you describe the overall atmosphere at work? Is it generally positive or negative? Please provide specific examples if possible.
2. Do people in your organization feel comfortable expressing their opinions and ideas, even when they differ from those of management or other team members? Can employees suggest new initiatives without fear of being shut down because "this is the way we've always done it"? Is there a mechanism for capturing these suggestions to evaluate them more rigorously later on if necessary.
3. Do you think that your company has an inclusive culture, where everyone feels welcome and valued? Are all employees treated with respect regardless of their background or position in the organization hierarchy ? If not then what steps can be taken so as make it a little bit better place for people from different walks life . Please elaborate on this question.
4. Is there open communication between management/HR department & other staff members about important decisions that affect everyone's daily lives at work? Or do you feel like things are decided behind closed doors and then announced without any room left over to give feedback or ask questions ? If yes, what kind of information is shared openly with employees.
5. Do people in your organization have the resources they need (technology/time)to perform their jobs effectively; if not do you think this impacts overall culture negatively? Please explain how lack /availability can be improved . 6: Does management team show appreciation for hard work and dedication of employees through words or actions, like giving bonuses , time offs etc. If yes then what methods are used to acknowledge good performance ?
7 Do you feel that your company values diversity in terms of ideas as well? Are there opportunities available equally regardless whether someone is coming from different background/culture and has unique perspective on things compared with others who might be more traditional or similar minded . Please elaborate. 8: Is it easy for newcomers to integrate into the team, do they receive necessary support & guidance so that can perform well quickly without feeling overwhelmed by existing workload? If not then what could make this process smoother ?
9 How often does your company organizes events outside of regular working hours which help build relationships between colleagues and strengthens sense belongingness towards organization. Please specify types if any such activities are organized . 10: Is there a clear distinction made in workplace culture about right & wrong behavior, with consistent consequences for those who behave badly? If not then how can this be improved so that everyone understands what is expected of them ?
Please let me know whether you would like to add or remove any questions. I am happy help further if required .

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a potential questionnaire about workplace culture:
1. How would you describe the overall atmosphere at work? Is it generally positive or negative? Please provide specific examples if possible.
2. Do employees feel comfortable being themselves and expressing their opinions, even if they differ from those in leadership positions? Can you give an example of a time when someone felt uncomfortable sharing something because of backlash received for doing so previously? If yes, how did management address this issue to make the employee more comfortable moving forward.
3. Is there open communication between all levels and departments or is it difficult to get in touch with certain people/positions due to hierarchy barriers etcetera (please provide examples)? How does your company encourage transparency within teams? 4) Do you feel that management cares about their employees' well-being, both physically AND mentally OR are there instances where this has not been the case and what steps were taken if any.
5. Is turnover rate relatively low compared to industry standards or is it higher than average due perhaps even unrelated reasons? If so please explain why you believe that might be happening as well potential solutions for reducing high-turn over rates in future years should this apply at all! 6) How often do employees feel like they can speak up about issues without fear of punishment, retribution or other negative consequences associated with bringing attention to certain topics? Are there any specific instances where someone was punished simply because he/she voiced concern too loudly and frequently than others around him did not approve.
7) Is it easy for new hires (particularly those who may be introverted by nature or just less outgoing naturally)to fit into the current company culture, especially when first starting? Are there any programs in place to help onboarding process go more smoothly and make everyone feel welcome regardless of background/preferences etcetera.
8. Is it easy for new hires (particularly those who may be introverted by nature or just less outgoing naturally)to fit into the current company culture, especially when first starting? Are there any programs in place to help onboarding process go more smoothly and make everyone feel welcome regardless of background/preferences etcetera.
9. How does your organization handle conflict resolution between team members whether same department or different ones involved as well who might have conflicting personalities, work styles OR other issues unrelated directly but still important to address timely manner? Please share specific instances if possible and how they were handled by management/HR teams alike!
10. Is there a strong sense of community within the organization where everyone feels included regardless not just those in power positions or certain cliques, etcetera?? Can you give examples from personal experience working here about times when people came together despite differences initially but ultimately became better teammates due to shared values and goals?
11. Is there a strong sense of community within the organization where everyone feels included regardless not just those in power positions or certain cliques, etcetera?? Can you give examples from personal experience working here about times when people came together despite differences initially but ultimately became better teammates due to shared values and goals?
Please let me know if there are any specific formats that this questionnaire needs converted into. I will be happy make necessary adjustments!
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Culture

 Sure! Here is a potential questionnaire about workplace culture:

1. How would you describe the overall atmosphere at work? Is it generally positive or negative? Please provide specific examples if possible.
2. Do employees feel comfortable expressing their opinions and ideas, even when they differ from those in management positions? Can you give an example of a time this has happened recently?
3. Are there clear guidelines for how to behave towards colleagues that are fair but also flexible enough so people can be themselves at work without fear or favoritism playing too big role ? If yes then please specify what these rules/guidelines include . Otherwise why not and consequences if someone breaks them accidentally OR ON PURPOSE?
4. How often do you see supervisors, managers AND other leaders engaging with team members beyond just professional conversations but also as people who share common interests or hobbies outside of work environment ? If this doesn't happen frequently then what could be reasons behind it and how can we change that to make everyone feel more included in company culture?
5. Is there a sense of community within your organization, where all employees are encouraged AND motivated TO contribute ideas for improvement regardless if they will directly benefit them or not ? If yes please elaborate on process through which these suggestions get implemented into daily operations . Otherwise why is that and how can we implement it effectively without causing any harm?
6. Do you think there's enough support provided to help employees maintain work-life balance, especially during high pressure times like deadlines etc.. Please share your thoughts about this topic including potential solutions if not already present in company culture . If yes then what makes them successful and how can we replicate same success across all departments?
7. Is there a feeling of transparency within the organization where everyone knows (or at least has right to know) why certain decisions get made, even when those choices might affect their jobs negatively ? Can you give an example from your personal experience about time this happened and how it was handled by people involved in decision making process?
8. How often do employees feel like they're being heard within the company culture - both through communication channels AND during meetings where decisions get finalized without much input expected but still allowed ? If not then what could be reasons behind that feeling of disconnect and how can we bridge this gap effectively so everyone feels included in conversation regardless tenure or position level?
9. Is there a system for recognizing good work publicly within the organization, whether it's through an employee-of-the month program OR other methods which promote positivity among team members while also making sure that those who deserve recognition get acknowledged properly ? If not then why and how can we implement such practice without causing any harm?
10. Finally do you feel like there is a strong sense of inclusiveness within your organization, where everyone feels welcome regardless their backgrounds or personal preferences as long AS they respect others' rights too AND follow general rules set by company culture ? If not then what could be reasons behind that feeling and how can we change it to make every single person feel more comfortable at work?
Please let me know if you need any further clarification about these questions. I am happy to help!
