[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure thing! Here is a potential questionnaire about workplace environment:

1. How would you describe the physical working space? Is it comfortable, well-lit, quiet enough for focused work and spacious or cramped with little room to move around in? Please rate from 0 (not at all) to 5(very much).
2. Do your colleagues respect personal workspace boundaries like not using someone's desk as a throughway without permission etc., on scale of 1-7, where one is strongly disagree and seven represents strong agreement with statement "Colleagues are mindful about my working space"?
3. Is there enough storage room for files/equipment in your opinion? Please answer yes or no to question: Are you satisfied that all necessary things can be stored without cluttering the place, on scale of 0 (not at all) and 5(very much). If neutral - please specify what is missing.
4. Do YOU feel comfortable with temperature settings in your workspace? Please rate from 1 to 7 where one means strongly disagree that current setting could be improved while seven indicates strong agreement, it's perfect as-is! Temperature comfort can also include humidity and air quality if applicable - please specify what you find uncomfortable.
5. How do YOU feel about cleanliness of your working environment? Is there a regular cleaning schedule or does everything seem to be covered in dust after just few days, on scale 0(not at all) –-7 (strongly agree)? If neutral --please explain how often and with what tools things should ideally get cleaned.
6. Can you tell me if workplace environment is conducive for creativity? Is there a place where people can brainstorm together or have quiet spaces when they need them, on scale 0(not at all) –-7 (strongly agree)? If neutral --please explain what would make it better!
7. How do YOU feel about availability of resources like stationery items and technology in your workplace? Is there everything you personally require to perform job efficiently or is something missing, on scale 0(not at all) –-5 (strongly agree)? If neutral --please explain what would make it better!
8. Can You tell me if colleagues are supportive of each other's work and projects in your opinion? Please rate from one to seven where you strongly disagree that people help out when needed, up until 7 - they always lend a hand or share expertise generously with others around them on this scale (strongly agree). If neutral --please explain what would make it better!
9. Is there any evidence of discrimination in your workplace? Please answer yes/no to question: Do you feel that certain people are treated differently based solely upon their race, gender or age etc., and if so how does management team address this issue with staff members (scale 0(not at all) –-7 strongly agree)?
10. Can You tell me about level of collaboration in your workplace? Is there a sense that everyone works together towards common goals on scale from one to seven where you disagree or feel like people are isolated and not working as team, if neutral --please explain what would make it better!

The questions are all multiple choice, with the answer being either "Yes" or "No". The display order of the questions is 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7.

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a potential questionnaire about workplace environment:
1. How would you describe the overall physical condition of your current workspace? (e.g., temperature, lighting, cleanliness)
2. Do you feel comfortable bringing personal items to decorate or customize your work area? Why/Why not?
3. Is there enough storage space for supplies and materials in your workplace? If not, what is lacking?
4. How often do the office spaces get cleaned professionally by a cleaning service company ? And how about meeting rooms that are used frequently to host clients or employees from different departments of organization . Do you think it's sufficient according with number people who work here and frequency they use these areas for meetings etc ....?
5. Is there any specific type/style design theme which is preferred by management in your company ? If yes, what are the benefits that come along side this particular style or look of office space as per employees perspective . And if not then how it affects overall work environment and productivity level among team members who share same workspace with each other?
6. How does noise levels affect you while working at our organization: (either from people talking, machines running in background) Is there any way to reduce this problem or is everyone satisfied including yourself about current situation ? And how it affects your performance and productivity level on daily basis if not then what are the possible solutions which can be implemented by management team so that noise levels get reduced significantly without affecting overall workflow of organization?
7. How do you feel when working in an open office environment with no cubicles or partitions separating individual desks from each other ? And how it affects your performance and productivity level on daily basis if not then what are the possible solutions which can be implemented by management team so that everyone feels comfortable while sitting at their workspaces without any distractions around them?
8. How do you feel about current seating arrangements in office space where people have to sit close together due lack of available chairs or desks according with number employees who are working here currently ? And how it affects your performance and productivity level on daily basis if not then what are the possible solutions which can be implemented by management team so that everyone feels comfortable while sitting at their workspaces without any distractions around them?
9. How do you feel about current temperature settings in office space, especially during winter season when some people might prefer to have it little warmer than others due health issues or just personal preference ? And how it affects your performance and productivity level on daily basis if not then what are the possible solutions which can be implemented by management team so that everyone feels comfortable while sitting at their workspaces without any distractions around them?
10. How do you feel about current lighting conditions in office space, especially during daytime when some people might prefer to have it little brighter than others due health issues or just personal preference ? And how it affects your performance and productivity level on daily basis if not then what are the possible solutions which can be implemented by management team so that everyone feels comfortable while sitting at their workspaces without any distractions around them?
10 questions in total. I hope this helps you gather information about workplace environment for further analysis! Let me know, please If there is anything else or if my service was not upto the mark then do let me improve myself next time . Thank You !
     - User:

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator that helps HR users investigate phenomena within the company.
Firstly, the user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic.
Then, the user will ask to convert it into a specified format.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Environment

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure thing! Here is a potential questionnaire about workplace environment:

1. How would you describe the physical working space? Is it comfortable, well-lit, quiet enough for focused work and easily accessible by public transport or car if needed? Please rate from 0 to 5 (with five being best).
2. Do your colleagues create a positive atmosphere at workplace with their behavior towards each other as well as you personally ? Are they supportive in terms of sharing knowledge about tasks, helping out when there is need for it and encouraging others even outside work-related topics? Please rate from 0 to5 (with five being best).
3. Is the company culture open where everyone can share ideas without fear or favoritism based on position level within organization ? Can you easily approach your superiors if needed, including HR department about any issues that might arise in this area and feel comfortable discussing them? Please rate from 0 to5 (with five being best).
4. Are there opportunities for professional growth through training sessions provided by employer or other means such as mentoring program where junior employees can learn more advanced skills required at higher positions within company structure ? Can you tell us if these programs exist and how often they are held, then rate from 0 to5 (with five being best).
5. Is there a system in place which allows all staff members including yourself feel safe during work hours with clear guidelines about what is allowed behavior-wise towards others regardless of position level within organization ? Can you share information whether this kind environment exists and if yes, how does it function? Please rate from 0 to5 (with five being best).
6. How well do the company values align with your personal beliefs when considering social issues beyond just business operations but also community involvement activities supported by employer through financial means or time commitment ? Can you tell us whether this match exists and if not, how would that make YOU feel? Please rate from 0 to5 (with five being best).
7. Is there a sense of belonging within the company where everyone feels included regardless position level held inside organization structure including those who may be different in terms religion/ethnicity etc., or do people tend stick mostly with their own kind due various reasons? Can you share information whether this inclusive environment exists and if not, how would that make YOU feel ? Please rate from 0 to5 (with five being best).
8. Is there a good work-life balance encouraged within the company through flexible working hours or other means such as possibility of remote job for some positions? Can you tell us whether this kind environment exists and if not, how would that make YOU feel ? Please rate from 0 to5 (with five being best).
9. Is there a feeling like at home when entering workplace every day due good relationships between employees regardless position level held inside organization structure including those who may be different in terms religion/ethnicity etc., or do people tend stick mostly with their own kind? Can you share information whether this inclusive environment exists and if not, how would that make YOU feel ? Please rate from 0 to5 (with five being best).
10. Finally - is there a general sense of happiness within the company where everyone feels content about place they work at including satisfaction with salary level provided by employer? Can you tell us whether this kind environment exists and if not, how would that make YOU feel ? Please rate from 0 to5 (with five being best).
Please let me know when I can stop asking these questions. Thank You!
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Environment
